-moz-box-shadow: 0 1px 0 rgba(255,255,255,0.67),inset 0 1px 3px rgba(5,5,5,0.13);
box-shadow: 0 1px 0 rgba(255,255,255,0.67),inset 0 1px 3px rgba(5,5,5,0.13);
-webkit-border-radius: 3px;
-moz-border-radius: 3px;
border-radius: 3px;
box-sizing:border-box;
-moz-box-sizing:border-box;
height:auto;
}
#popup-box-sxzw-1 .popupally-inner-sxzw-1 .popupally-center-sxzw .content-sxzw input[type="submit"].submit-sxzw,
#popup-embedded-box-sxzw-1 .popupally-inner-sxzw-1 .popupally-center-sxzw .content-sxzw input[type="submit"].submit-sxzw{
font-family: Arial, Helvetica, sans-serif;
font-size: 22px;
line-height:27px;
background-color:#56b2bf;
border-style: solid;
border-width: 1pt;
border-color:#C0C0C0;
-webkit-box-sizing: border-box;
-moz-box-sizing: border-box;
box-sizing: border-box;
color:#ffffff;
text-shadow: 0 0.1em 0.3em rgba(0,0,0,0.3);
cursor: pointer;
-webkit-border-radius: 3pt;
-moz-border-radius: 3pt;

width:100%;
padding:15px 0;
margin: 10px auto;

-moz-box-sizing:border-box;
height:auto;

}
#popup-box-sxzw-1 .popupally-inner-sxzw-1 .popupally-center-sxzw .content-sxzw input[type="submit"].submit-sxzw:hover,
#popup-embedded-box-sxzw-1 .popupally-inner-sxzw-1 .popupally-center-sxzw .content-sxzw input[type="submit"].submit-sxzw:hover{

}
#popup-box-sxzw-1 .popupally-inner-sxzw-1 .privacy-sxzw,
#popup-embedded-box-sxzw-1 .popupally-inner-sxzw-1 .privacy-sxzw{

font-size:14px;
line-height:14px;
color:#444444;
display: block;
margin:10px 0;
padding:0;

-moz-box-sizing:border-box;
}

}

}

}

#popup-box-sxzw-1 .popupally-inner-sxzw-1 .logo-text-sxzw,
#popup-embedded-box-sxzw-1 .popupally-inner-sxzw-1 .logo-text-sxzw{

}

	#popup-box-sxzw-1 .popupally-inner-sxzw-1 .popupally-center-sxzw .content-sxzw input[type="text"].field-sxzw, #popup-embedded-box-sxzw-1 .popupally-inner-sxzw-1 .popupally-center-sxzw .content-sxzw input[type="text"].field-sxzw {padding:10px 10px;font-size: 12px;line-height: 18px;margin-bottom:7px;}
	#popup-box-sxzw-1 .popupally-inner-sxzw-1 .popupally-center-sxzw .content-sxzw input[type="submit"].submit-sxzw, #popup-embedded-box-sxzw-1 .popupally-inner-sxzw-1 .popupally-center-sxzw .content-sxzw input[type="submit"].submit-sxzw {font-size: 18px;padding:10px 0;margin-top:8px;margin-bottom:8px;}
	#popup-box-sxzw-1 .popupally-inner-sxzw-1 .privacy-sxzw, #popup-embedded-box-sxzw-1 .popupally-inner-sxzw-1 .privacy-sxzw{font-size:10px;line-height:10px;}
	#popup-box-sxzw-1 .popupally-inner-sxzw-1 .logo-row-sxzw, #popup-embedded-box-sxzw-1 .popupally-inner-sxzw-1 .logo-row-sxzw {margin:15px 0;}
	#popup-box-sxzw-1 .popupally-inner-sxzw-1 .logo-img-sxzw, #popup-embedded-box-sxzw-1 .popupally-inner-sxzw-1 .logo-img-sxzw {height:80px;margin:0 15px 0 0;}
	#popup-box-sxzw-1 .popupally-inner-sxzw-1 .logo-text-sxzw, #popup-embedded-box-sxzw-1 .popupally-inner-sxzw-1 .logo-text-sxzw {font-size:20px;line-height:22px;}
}
@media (max-width: 520px) {

	#popup-embedded-box-sxzw-1.popupally-outer-embedded-sxzw-1{width:300px;}
	#popup-box-sxzw-1 .popupally-inner-sxzw-1 .desc-sxzw, #popup-embedded-box-sxzw-1 .popupally-inner-sxzw-1 .desc-sxzw{font-size:18px;line-height:20px;}
	#popup-box-sxzw-1 .popupally-inner-sxzw-1 .popupally-center-sxzw .content-sxzw input[type="text"].field-sxzw, #popup-embedded-box-sxzw-1 .popupally-inner-sxzw-1 .popupally-center-sxzw .content-sxzw input[type="text"].field-sxzw {padding:10px 6px;font-size: 10px;line-height: 14px;margin-bottom:5px;}
	#popup-box-sxzw-1 .popupally-inner-sxzw-1 .popupally-center-sxzw .content-sxzw input[type="submit"].submit-sxzw, #popup-embedded-box-sxzw-1 .popupally-inner-sxzw-1 .popupally-center-sxzw .content-sxzw input[type="submit"].submit-sxzw {font-size: 16px;padding:8px 0;margin-top:4px;margin-bottom:4px;}
	#popup-box-sxzw-1 .popupally-inner-sxzw-1 .privacy-sxzw, #popup-embedded-box-sxzw-1 .popupally-inner-sxzw-1 .privacy-sxzw{font-size:8px;line-height:8px;}
	#popup-box-sxzw-1 .popupally-inner-sxzw-1 .logo-row-sxzw, #popup-embedded-box-sxzw-1 .popupally-inner-sxzw-1 .logo-row-sxzw {margin:10px 0;}
	#popup-box-sxzw-1 .popupally-inner-sxzw-1 .logo-img-sxzw, #popup-embedded-box-sxzw-1 .popupally-inner-sxzw-1 .logo-img-sxzw {height:60px;margin:0 10px 0 0;}
	#popup-box-sxzw-1 .popupally-inner-sxzw-1 .logo-text-sxzw, #popup-embedded-box-sxzw-1 .popupally-inner-sxzw-1 .logo-text-sxzw {font-size:12px;line-height:14px;}
}

    <div class="content-sidebar-wrap">
     <main class="content" itemprop="mainContentOfPage" itemscope="itemscope" itemtype="http://schema.org/Blog" role="main">
      <article class="post-397 post type-post status-publish format-standard has-post-thumbnail category-burlap category-decorating category-how-to tag-laundry entry" itemprop="blogPost" itemscope="itemscope" itemtype="http://schema.org/BlogPosting">
       <header class="entry-header">
        <h1 class="entry-title" itemprop="headline">
         Burlap Laundry SignHow to!
        </h1>
        <p class="entry-meta">
         <time class="entry-time" datetime="2010-09-24T00:33:00+00:00" itemprop="datePublished">
          September 24, 2010
         </time>
         By
         <span class="entry-author" itemprop="author" itemscope="itemscope" itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
          <a class="entry-author-link" href="http://www.domestically-speaking.com/author/domesticallyspeaking" itemprop="url" rel="author">
           <span class="entry-author-name" itemprop="name">
            Maryann @ Domestically Speaking
           </span>
          </a>
         </span>
         <span class="entry-comments-link">
          <a href="http://www.domestically-speaking.com/2010/09/burlap-laundry-signhow-to.html#comments">
           161 Comments
          </a>
         </span>
        </p>
       </header>
       <div class="entry-content" itemprop="text">
        <div class="shareaholic-canvas" data-app="share_buttons" data-app-id="5531496" data-link="http://www.domestically-speaking.com/2010/09/burlap-laundry-signhow-to.html" data-summary="" data-title="Burlap Laundry SignHow to!">
        </div>
        <div align="center">
        </div>
        <div align="center">
         <a href="http://lh3.ggpht.com/_G5_YGMiglIw/TJwq2OOK2vI/AAAAAAAACYA/5wYVe8__0jo/s1600-h/burlap%20laundry%20sign%2011%5B4%5D.jpg" onclick="_gaq.push(['_trackEvent', 'outbound-article', 'http://lh3.ggpht.com/_G5_YGMiglIw/TJwq2OOK2vI/AAAAAAAACYA/5wYVe8__0jo/s1600-h/burlap%20laundry%20sign%2011%5B4%5D.jpg', '']);">
          <span style="color: #333333; font-family: Gabriola; font-size: large;">
           <img alt="" border="0" height="820" src="http://lh6.ggpht.com/_G5_YGMiglIw/TJwq2rl7cMI/AAAAAAAACYE/pQKpcrcqw_w/burlap%20laundry%20sign%2011_thumb%5B2%5D.jpg?imgmax=800" style="display: inline; border: 0px;" title="" width="620"/>
          </span>
         </a>
        </div>
        <div align="center">
         <span style="font-family: Gabriola; font-size: large;">
          So I
          <span style="text-decoration: underline;">
           finally
          </span>
          got my hands on freezer paper!
         </span>
        </div>
        <div align="center">
         <span style="font-family: Gabriola; font-size: large;">
          I figured I would
          <em>
           <strong>
            try
           </strong>
          </em>
          to use my freezer paper to print on some burlap did you know you can print on material with some printers?
         </span>
        </div>
        <div align="center">
         <span style="font-family: Gabriola; font-size: large;">
          <strong>
           {1st Step}
          </strong>
         </span>
        </div>
        <div align="center">
         <span style="font-family: Gabriola; font-size: large;">
          I created my laundry verbiage in Photoshop elements, but you could use any word processing program. I made it 8 1/2 x 11, so that it would run through my printer as a standard piece of paper. I went to an online dictionary to find the definition I used.
         </span>
        </div>
        <div align="center">
         <span style="font-family: Gabriola; font-size: large;">
          <strong>
           {2nd Step}
          </strong>
         </span>
        </div>
        <div align="center">
         <a href="http://lh6.ggpht.com/_G5_YGMiglIw/TJwq24La0II/AAAAAAAACYI/-vrH5a0Fe1E/s1600-h/burlaplaundrysign14.jpg" onclick="_gaq.push(['_trackEvent', 'outbound-article', 'http://lh6.ggpht.com/_G5_YGMiglIw/TJwq24La0II/AAAAAAAACYI/-vrH5a0Fe1E/s1600-h/burlaplaundrysign14.jpg', '']);">
          <span style="color: #333333; font-family: Gabriola; font-size: large;">
           <img alt="" border="0" height="553" src="http://lh4.ggpht.com/_G5_YGMiglIw/TJwq3IhreKI/AAAAAAAACYM/56yvgixj8F8/burlaplaundrysign1_thumb2.jpg?imgmax=800" style="display: inline; border-width: 0px;" title="" width="420"/>
          </span>
         </a>
        </div>
        <div align="center">
         <span style="font-family: Gabriola; font-size: large;">
          Iron the burlap.
         </span>
        </div>
        <div align="center">
         <span style="font-family: Gabriola; font-size: large;">
          I had a piece of scrap burlap that worked perfectly for this project. You want your fabric nice and smooth for the printing.
         </span>
        </div>
        <div align="center">
         <span style="font-family: Gabriola; font-size: large;">
          <strong>
           {3rd Step}
          </strong>
         </span>
        </div>
        <div align="center">
         <a href="http://lh4.ggpht.com/_G5_YGMiglIw/TJwq3fH6MyI/AAAAAAAACYQ/CyK8AlrE9uY/s1600-h/burlaplaundrysign24.jpg" onclick="_gaq.push(['_trackEvent', 'outbound-article', 'http://lh4.ggpht.com/_G5_YGMiglIw/TJwq3fH6MyI/AAAAAAAACYQ/CyK8AlrE9uY/s1600-h/burlaplaundrysign24.jpg', '']);">
          <span style="color: #333333; font-family: Gabriola; font-size: large;">
           <img alt="" border="0" height="432" src="http://lh3.ggpht.com/_G5_YGMiglIw/TJwq3sLYoOI/AAAAAAAACYU/iKWQSuFuquw/burlaplaundrysign2_thumb2.jpg?imgmax=800" style="display: inline; border-width: 0px;" title="" width="570"/>
          </span>
         </a>
        </div>
        <div align="center">
         <span style="font-family: Gabriola; font-size: large;">
          Place your freezer paper on top of your ironed burlap with the shiny side down (touching the burlap). Run a medium, dry iron on top of the freezer paper and it will
          <em>
           magically
          </em>
          adhere to your burlap.
         </span>
        </div>
        <div align="center">
         <span style="font-family: Gabriola; font-size: large;">
          <strong>
           {4th Step}
          </strong>
         </span>
        </div>
        <div align="center">
         <a href="http://lh6.ggpht.com/_G5_YGMiglIw/TJwq36SGVPI/AAAAAAAACYY/vng8VsjG104/s1600-h/burlaplaundrysign34.jpg" onclick="_gaq.push(['_trackEvent', 'outbound-article', 'http://lh6.ggpht.com/_G5_YGMiglIw/TJwq36SGVPI/AAAAAAAACYY/vng8VsjG104/s1600-h/burlaplaundrysign34.jpg', '']);">
          <span style="color: #333333; font-family: Gabriola; font-size: large;">
           <img alt="" border="0" height="488" src="http://lh5.ggpht.com/_G5_YGMiglIw/TJwq4GYIbPI/AAAAAAAACYc/rsz13fVge3w/burlaplaundrysign3_thumb2.jpg?imgmax=800" style="display: inline; border-width: 0px;" title="" width="420"/>
          </span>
         </a>
        </div>
        <div align="center">
         <span style="font-family: Gabriola; font-size: large;">
          Cut your burlap/freezer paper into your 8 1/2 x 11 size.
         </span>
        </div>
        <div align="center">
         <span style="font-family: Gabriola; font-size: large;">
          <strong>
           {5th Step}
          </strong>
         </span>
        </div>
        <div align="center">
         <a href="http://lh4.ggpht.com/_G5_YGMiglIw/TJwq4chCJDI/AAAAAAAACYg/m1jBS43SwAw/s1600-h/burlaplaundrysign44.jpg" onclick="_gaq.push(['_trackEvent', 'outbound-article', 'http://lh4.ggpht.com/_G5_YGMiglIw/TJwq4chCJDI/AAAAAAAACYg/m1jBS43SwAw/s1600-h/burlaplaundrysign44.jpg', '']);">
          <span style="color: #333333; font-family: Gabriola; font-size: large;">
           <img alt="" border="0" height="470" src="http://lh5.ggpht.com/_G5_YGMiglIw/TJwq44N1ZiI/AAAAAAAACYk/lELmPbnlnAM/burlaplaundrysign4_thumb2.jpg?imgmax=800" style="display: inline; border-width: 0px;" title="" width="620"/>
          </span>
         </a>
        </div>
        <div align="center">
         <span style="font-family: Gabriola; font-size: large;">
          Run your burlap/freezer paper through your printer.
         </span>
        </div>
        <div align="center">
         <span style="font-family: Gabriola; font-size: large;">
          <strong>
           {6th Step}
          </strong>
         </span>
        </div>
        <div align="center">
         <a href="http://lh5.ggpht.com/_G5_YGMiglIw/TJwq5OQ4vaI/AAAAAAAACYo/DOs0qiOfKO8/s1600-h/burlaplaundrysign54.jpg" onclick="_gaq.push(['_trackEvent', 'outbound-article', 'http://lh5.ggpht.com/_G5_YGMiglIw/TJwq5OQ4vaI/AAAAAAAACYo/DOs0qiOfKO8/s1600-h/burlaplaundrysign54.jpg', '']);">
          <span style="color: #333333; font-family: Gabriola; font-size: large;">
           <img alt="" border="0" height="432" src="http://lh4.ggpht.com/_G5_YGMiglIw/TJwq5QhujdI/AAAAAAAACYs/Z21WJUqjAs8/burlaplaundrysign5_thumb2.jpg?imgmax=800" style="display: inline; border-width: 0px;" title="" width="570"/>
          </span>
         </a>
        </div>
        <div align="center">
         <span style="font-family: Gabriola; font-size: large;">
          Peel off the freezer paper.
         </span>
        </div>
        <div align="center">
         <span style="font-family: Gabriola; font-size: large;">
          and you have this amazing printed burlap!
         </span>
        </div>
        <div align="center">
         <a href="http://lh5.ggpht.com/_G5_YGMiglIw/TJwq5qAuHlI/AAAAAAAACYw/HSJCTPyQEN0/s1600-h/burlap%20laundry%20sign%207%5B4%5D.jpg" onclick="_gaq.push(['_trackEvent', 'outbound-article', 'http://lh5.ggpht.com/_G5_YGMiglIw/TJwq5qAuHlI/AAAAAAAACYw/HSJCTPyQEN0/s1600-h/burlap%20laundry%20sign%207%5B4%5D.jpg', '']);">
          <span style="color: #333333; font-family: Gabriola; font-size: large;">
           <img alt="" border="0" height="696" src="http://lh5.ggpht.com/_G5_YGMiglIw/TJwq6FZEuMI/AAAAAAAACY0/74Kyk3pPqHM/burlap%20laundry%20sign%207_thumb%5B2%5D.jpg?imgmax=800" style="display: inline; border: 0px;" title="" width="620"/>
          </span>
         </a>
        </div>
        <div align="center">
         <span style="font-family: Gabriola; font-size: large;">
          To finish off this project, I used the leftovers of the foam board from my
          <a href="http://www.domestically-speaking.com/2010/08/check-your-pockets-laundry-fun.html">
           Check My Pockets laundry sign
          </a>
          to create the backing for my empty black frame.
         </span>
        </div>
        <div align="center">
         <a href="http://lh4.ggpht.com/_G5_YGMiglIw/TJwq6TT22BI/AAAAAAAACY4/WI0IwAlEj6E/s1600-h/burlap%20laundry%20sign%2010%5B4%5D.jpg" onclick="_gaq.push(['_trackEvent', 'outbound-article', 'http://lh4.ggpht.com/_G5_YGMiglIw/TJwq6TT22BI/AAAAAAAACY4/WI0IwAlEj6E/s1600-h/burlap%20laundry%20sign%2010%5B4%5D.jpg', '']);">
          <span style="color: #333333; font-family: Gabriola; font-size: large;">
           <img alt="" border="0" height="470" src="http://lh4.ggpht.com/_G5_YGMiglIw/TJwq6kTx2UI/AAAAAAAACY8/hKbSPa2SESI/burlap%20laundry%20sign%2010_thumb%5B2%5D.jpg?imgmax=800" style="display: inline; border: 0px;" title="" width="620"/>
          </span>
         </a>
        </div>
        <div align="center">
         <span style="font-family: Gabriola; font-size: large;">
          To adhere the burlap sign I used decorative nails.
         </span>
        </div>
        <div align="center">
         <a href="http://lh5.ggpht.com/_G5_YGMiglIw/TJwq61KNkaI/AAAAAAAACZA/BSeWe7Hg2ow/s1600-h/burlap%20laundry%20sign%208%5B4%5D.jpg" onclick="_gaq.push(['_trackEvent', 'outbound-article', 'http://lh5.ggpht.com/_G5_YGMiglIw/TJwq61KNkaI/AAAAAAAACZA/BSeWe7Hg2ow/s1600-h/burlap%20laundry%20sign%208%5B4%5D.jpg', '']);">
          <span style="color: #333333; font-family: Gabriola; font-size: large;">
           <img alt="" border="0" height="490" src="http://lh6.ggpht.com/_G5_YGMiglIw/TJwq7ZnUFEI/AAAAAAAACZE/qV8Lw2PWyXA/burlap%20laundry%20sign%208_thumb%5B2%5D.jpg?imgmax=800" style="display: inline; border: 0px;" title="" width="620"/>
          </span>
         </a>
        </div>
        <div align="center">
         <span style="font-family: Gabriola; font-size: large;">
          I used scraps of burlap, remnants of a
          <a href="http://www.domestically-speaking.com/2010/02/wasting-no-sweater-scrapsneck-roll.html">
           sweater I turned into a pillow
          </a>
          and the remains of my
          <a href="http://www.domestically-speaking.com/2010/07/frilly-dress-turned-frilly-pillow.html">
           daughters dress turned pillow
          </a>
           and twisted and hot glued them onto felt to create some cute flowers. I glued the flowers onto the foam board and frame with my trusty hot glue gun.
         </span>
        </div>
        <div align="center">
         <a href="http://lh3.ggpht.com/_G5_YGMiglIw/TJwq7lQg-tI/AAAAAAAACZI/4fSkqW9OTSg/s1600-h/burlap%20laundry%20sign%206%5B4%5D.jpg" onclick="_gaq.push(['_trackEvent', 'outbound-article', 'http://lh3.ggpht.com/_G5_YGMiglIw/TJwq7lQg-tI/AAAAAAAACZI/4fSkqW9OTSg/s1600-h/burlap%20laundry%20sign%206%5B4%5D.jpg', '']);">
          <span style="color: #333333; font-family: Gabriola; font-size: large;">
           <img alt="" border="0" height="642" src="http://lh5.ggpht.com/_G5_YGMiglIw/TJwq752lteI/AAAAAAAACZM/C7Hc6MyAAJ0/burlap%20laundry%20sign%206_thumb%5B2%5D.jpg?imgmax=800" style="display: inline; border: 0px;" title="" width="520"/>
          </span>
         </a>
        </div>
        <div align="center">
         <span style="font-family: Gabriola; font-size: large;">
          My newest laundry love!
         </span>
        </div>
        <div align="center">
         <span style="font-family: Gabriola; font-size: large;">
          ~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~
         </span>
        </div>
        <div align="center">
         <span style="font-family: Gabriola; font-size: large;">
          Sharing my how-to in the fab parties in my PARTIES menu bar button!
         </span>
        </div>
        <div align="center">
        </div>
        <div align="center">
        </div>
        <p>
         <a href="http://www.domestically-speaking.com/wp-content/uploads/2010/09/Learn-How-to-Print-on-Burlap.jpg">
          <img alt="Learn How to Print on Burlap" class="aligncenter size-large wp-image-11565" height="1024" src="http://www.domestically-speaking.com/wp-content/uploads/2010/09/Learn-How-to-Print-on-Burlap-446x1024.jpg" width="446"/>
         </a>
        </p>

          <header class="comment-header">
           <p class="comment-author" itemprop="creator" itemscope="itemscope" itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">

           <p class="comment-meta">
            <time class="comment-time" datetime="2012-10-06T08:27:32+00:00" itemprop="commentTime">
             <a class="comment-time-link" href="http://www.domestically-speaking.com/2010/09/burlap-laundry-signhow-to.html#comment-58084" itemprop="url">
              October 6, 2012 at 8:27 am
             </a>
            </time>
           </p>
          </header>
          <div class="comment-content" itemprop="commentText">
           <p>
            I just did this and it worked the first time without any printer jamming!  I did hold my breath and squinted the whole time it printed though.  I designed it in Word (Im not software savvy) and followed the instructions above and ran it through an HP Photosmart 7510 Inkjet printer.  I originally did this on lighter burlap at the default normal setting and the ink smeared a bit.  It gave it character, but I had darker burlap and changed the setting to best quality and tried it again.  This time it came out much nicer.  So go with a darker burlap.  I have a laser printer, but its so sensitive Im afraid to try it.
           </p>
          </div>

             <p>
              You can find freezer paper in the same section in a store that has plastic wrap, aluminum foil, sandwich/food storage bags.  It will say freezer paper on it.  Also, it is NOT  the same as waxed paper, waxed paper is a different product altogether.  Hope that helped.. Im not sure if Im brave enough to try sendin something other than paper through my printer- mainly because Id never hear the end of it from my husband that might be the straw that broke the crafters  husbands back!

           <p>
            Which printers this for work for I really can't answer I'm not a printer expert.  I've got a cheap bubble jet printer and it worked great.  You want your burlap to be facing the direction it needs to in order to be printed on.  In my printer my burlap was facing up in the printer tray this is the side that gets printed on.  Hope that helps!
           </p>

               </a>
              </time>
